THE  UNITED  NATIONS  ACT,  No 45  OF  1968
Consolidated  List  under  Regulation  4 (2) (a) of the United Nations
Regulations No. 2 of 2012
THE Consolidated List of designated persons referred to in sub-paragraph (a) of paragraph (2) of regulation 4 of the United
Nations Regulations No. 2 of 2012 published in the Gazette Extraordinary No. 1760/40 of May 31, 2012, shall be as specified
in the Schedule hereto.
GOTABAY A RAJAPAKSA RWP, RSP, psc,
Secretary,
Ministry of Deffence & Urban Development.
Colombo,
07th June 2013.
